	<h1 class="hl ">
						The 2013 Corvette Convertible</h1>	
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						</div>
				</div>
</div>
<div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Drop the top in a Corvette convertible and completely unleash the  driving experience. Corvette defines freedom among luxury sports cars  with state-of-the-art technology and sleek, modern style. For 60 years,  Corvette has elevated the standard of excellence among sports cars and  earned its position as an icon.</p>
<p>Precision and excellence define Corvette convertible, from its standard 430-horsepower LS3 all-aluminum V8 engine to its <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_0" class="ln disclaimer_1">26-MPG-highway<sup>†</sup></a>  fuel efficiency. Along with a refined interior and options for  personalization, the 2013 Corvette convertible stands to reflect  unparalleled distinction. Yours.<br>
<br>
</p></div>
				<ul class="ull ui-layout-horizontal ui-layout-left"><li><div class="parbase download section"><a class="dl_pdf" href="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Corvette%20Convertible/Model%20Overview/PDFs/2013_Corvette_eBrochure.pdf" target="_blank" id="" title="Download Catalog">Download Catalog</a>
	</div>
</li><li><div class="parbase download section"><a class="dl_pdf" href="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Corvette%20Convertible/Model%20Overview/PDFs/2013_Corvette_SpecSheet.pdf" target="_blank" id="" title="Download Spec Sheet">Download Spec Sheet</a>
	</div>
</li></ul></div>
		</div></div>
</div>
</div></div>

		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<a href="/cars/2013-corvette-convertible/model-overview/candles.content.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-3col'});}" class="btn_lyr"><img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Corvette%20Convertible/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-corvette-convertible-model-overview-cnt_well_2-316x179-08.jpg" alt="" width="316" height="179" class="mm"/></a></div>

</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h3 class="pt">
					Corvette celebrates its 60-year history</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>To mark this milestone in the Corvette story, the Corvette 60th Anniversary Design Package will be available on all 2013 Corvette models. Showcased here on the 2013 Corvette 427 Convertible, this package boasts an Arctic White exterior and a Blue Diamond leather-wrapped interior with sueded microfiber accents. The optional graphics package adds a classic track-ready appearance with full-length racing stripes in Pearl Silver Blue.<br>
</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h3 class="pt">
					</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>The stripes run the full length of the vehicle, including the interior in convertible models. The convertible top even continues the appearance with stitched stripes. The package also includes gray-painted brake calipers, a ZR1 rear spoiler and 60th Anniversary badging on the wheel center caps, steering wheel and seat head restraints to give a finishing touch to this sleek and distinctive appearance.<br>
</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</div><div class="mds-area-pf1"><div class="cnt_well_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_well_1 mds-cmp-content20" id="Performance">
	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_behind">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 1px; top: 130px; margin-bottom: 130px; margin-left: 11px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Corvette%20Convertible/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-corvette-convertible-model-overview-cnt_well_3-980x774-01.jpg" alt="" width="980" height="774" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					Performance</h2>
			<h3 class="pt">
					Power harnessed and finely tuned</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Corvette convertible is inspired by the speed and force echoing from the world’s most legendary racetracks, while remaining road ready. Its hydroformed steel structure gives Corvette its iconic shape and strength. It stabilizes the convertible so completely that no additional support is necessary, so relax and enjoy all of the performance Corvette has to offer</p>
<p>The standard 6.2-liter LS3 all-aluminum small block V8 engine powering the convertible produces 430 horsepower and 424 lb.-ft. of torque (436 horsepower and 428 lb.-ft. of torque with available dual-mode exhaust). And with its favorable power-to-weight ratio, Corvette convertible performs like a thoroughbred, with a 0 to 60 time of 4.2 seconds on the test track.</p>
<p>This all translates to off-track precision and performance, not to mention efficiency. Offering 26 MPG <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_0" class="ln disclaimer_1">highway</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_0" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup> with manual transmission, Corvette convertible boasts a better highway fuel economy than Porsche 911 Targa 4S, and equals many 6-cylinder sports cars, including <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_1" class="ln disclaimer_1">BMW Z4 ADrive35is</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_1" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup>.<br>
</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h3 class="pt">
					Suspension dialed to perfection</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Stiffen the suspension capability for winding roads while providing a more compliant ride for city and highway driving with available Magnetic Selective Ride Control™. An electromagnetic coil resides inside each damper piston. When an electrical current is applied—variably controlled by a microprocessor — ferrous particles in the shock fluid instantly bond, making the fluid more flow resistant, effectively stiffening the shock’s damping. Conversely, when the electromagnetic field is reduced, the fluid flows more freely, allowing easier suspension movement. Explore two cockpit settings — Tour and Sport.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p></div>
				</div></div>
<div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h3 class="pt">
					Launch control — power straight <br/>to pavement</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Put the pedal to the floor and let launch control take care of the rest. When there’s this much power, launch control is the perfect middleman between you and sheer bliss. Standard with the short-throw 6-speed manual gearbox, it modulates engine rpm in competitive mode to lay the power down more smoothly while providing consistent acceleration times on the test track. It’s a feature for those who like to compete in club-sanctioned closed-course track events, but may just tempt others to start.</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>
</div>

	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					Exterior</h2>
			<h3 class="pt">
					A top made for dropping</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>                    It’s a convertible for a reason, drop the top and let the natural air refresh your senses. Select either the standard manual top or the available power top that lets you raise the roof in 18 seconds, because we know you never want to leave the driver seat. Even with the top down, there’s still plenty of trunk space for anything, including two golf bags for those stressful business meetings. </p></div>
				</div></div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Classically aggressive exterior</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    Rounded fenders and a lean, grounded body frame are classic Corvette design elements that have been the foundation of its exterior design for nearly 60 years. Its unmistakable look makes it hard to resist and impossible to miss.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>

	<dl>

<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h3 class="pt">
					A refined interior, inch by inch</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>When the top is down in a Corvette convertible, there’s nothing separating you from the open air and natural light. The world is your interior in the mere 18 seconds it takes for the convertible’s roof to drop and stow away with the available power top — all without ever leaving the driver seat. When the world is your track, you shouldn’t have to get out of your seat to drop the top. Get even closer to your Corvette experience than ever.</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h3 class="pt">
					Luxury at every touch</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>The Corvette convertible interior has been refined for greater driving support and comfort. The seat design includes larger bolsters on the seatback and cushion areas for increased support, especially in high-performance driving, but greatly welcomed for day-to-day driving. Optional microfiber seat inserts complement the new design even further, as does the revised steering wheel featuring model-specific badges, streamlined switch trim, wrapped spokes, better hand placement and thumb grips.</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h3 class="pt">
					Excellence in every detail</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>No detail was overlooked in creating the most luxurious Corvette convertible interior to date. Padded center console and armrests on all models soften the interior, while the added visual touch of contrasting color stitching — in red, blue and yellow — is available with the Custom Leather-Wrapped Interior Package on the 4LT trim level. Driving a Corvette convertible is an experience for every one of your senses. Every interaction should remind you that you’re in a Corvette and it’s not like anything else.</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

		</dl>
	</div>
	</div>
</li><li><div class="cnt_btn_1 mod modCnt_btn_1 section mds-cmp-content02"><a href="/corvette-convertible/features-specs/trims.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'contentarea'});}" class="btn_sec"><span>See Features</span>
		</a></div>

</div><div class="mds-area-pf1"><div class="cnt_well_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_well_1 mds-cmp-content20">
	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="section grid_col1_c1"><div class="mds-area-pf1">
	<div class="pf1a_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					Technology</h2>
			</div></div>
<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Corvette%20Convertible/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-corvette-convertible-model-overview-cnt_well_1-980x316-22.jpg" alt="" width="980" height="316" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						Comfort, convenience and cutting edge</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Corvette convertible includes modern technology features that keep you connected to your life. For even more convenience, the Technology Package standard on the reconfigured 2LT brings together many of the most popular infotainment features such as navigation <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_2" class="ln disclaimer_1">radio</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_2" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup>, head-up display, Bose<sup>®</sup> premium audio system, SiriusXM Satellite <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">Radio</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup> services for one year, Bluetooth<sup>®</sup> wireless <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">technology</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup> for select phones and a USB <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_5" class="ln disclaimer_1">port<sup>†</sup></a>.</p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						Composite body panels</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>                    Technology is an all-inclusive feature in Corvette, down to every detail. Composite body panels used to form the exterior are stronger and lighter than other materials and help reduce the vehicle’s overall weight, and seriously increasing potential. The panels never rust, which keeps your Corvette looking as timeless as it is.</p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						Head-Up Display</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Keep important readings within sight while focusing on the road ahead with the optional Head-Up Display, including g-force meter. Utilizing proven technology, the display appears on the front windshield as if hovering above the front bumper, making it easier to read while driving. For differing driving styles, the display includes two modes — track and street, which also includes helpful Turn-by-Turn <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">Navigation</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup> through the navigation <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_2" class="ln disclaimer_1">system</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_2" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup>.</p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_4C_bose.png" alt="" width="92" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									The Power of Bose<sup>® </sup></span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Corvette offers a Bose Premium Audio System, which includes nine speakers for improved audio quality that is more precisely tuned to the cabin’s acoustics. Tweeters located in the instrument panel and improved Bose Nd<sup>®</sup> next-generation bass performance round out this truly premium audio experience.</p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_4C_bluetooth_small.png" alt="" width="127" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									wireless technology<sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup></span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Stay connected to your life while keeping your eyes on the road ahead of you. Take calls with just a touch of a button. That’s if you decide to — you may not because you’re so wrapped up in your Corvette convertible.</p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_4C_siriusxm.png" alt="" width="92" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									SiriusXM Satellite Radio<sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup></span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>                    Enjoy commercial-free music channels along with compelling talk, news, comedy, family programming and much more from coast to coast. Three-month subscription comes standard. One year of service included with 2LT, 3LT and 4LT. </p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>

	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					Experience Corvette</h2>
			</div></div>
<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Corvette%20Convertible/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-corvette-convertible-model-overview-cnt_well_1-980x476-23.jpg" alt="" width="980" height="476" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Get Schooled</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>There are two official Corvette Driving schools available to attend that can help you get the most enjoyment out of your Corvette. <a href="http://www.bondurant.com/?gclid=CLix57CF_KkCFUvCKgodPGaUYw" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.bondurant.com/?gclid=CLix57CF_KkCFUvCKgodPGaUYw');" target="_blank">Bob Bondurant School of High Performance Driving</a> in suburban Phoenix or the <a href="http://www.springmountainmotorsports.com/driving-schools/corvette-performance-driving-schools" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.springmountainmotorsports.com/driving-schools/corvette-performance-driving-schools');" target="_blank">Ron Fellows Performance Corvette Driving School</a> at Spring Mountain Motorsports Ranch near <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_9" class="ln disclaimer_1">Las Vegas<sup>†</sup></a>.</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05">
			<div class="inner">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Corvette%20Convertible/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-corvette-convertible-model-overview-cnt_well_7-462x320-02.png" alt="" width="462" height="320" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Add your distinctive mark</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    Individuality is a trademark of Corvette owners. You can make your Corvette even more of a personal statement with more than 50 available dealer-installed Genuine Corvette Accessories. Whether you’re looking to put your personal touch on the interior or exterior, there’s an assortment of accessories to match your style. From body-color engine covers to a cat-back exhaust with tips, all are designed to enhance the appearance or extend the functionality of your Corvette. To order your Accessories, visit your local dealer.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Corvette history is your history</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>A Corvette isn’t just a sports car; it’s a milestone — one that comes with a rich history and an exciting future. Corvette owners can become a part of that history by taking delivery of their vehicle right on the floor of the National Corvette Museum (NCM) in Bowling Green, Kentucky. NCM welcomes Corvette enthusiasts from all over the world and offers a variety of options for owners. Corvette museum delivery includes an NCM Delivery Team tour of the nearby Corvette Assembly Plant and a VIP museum <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_7" class="ln disclaimer_1">tour</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_7" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup>, as well as a quality orientation followed by a thorough delivery presentation of your new Corvette. Museum delivery is available to order through your Chevy dealer for an additional cost. <a href="http://www.corvettemuseum.org/" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.corvettemuseum.org/');" target="_blank">Visit the National Corvette Museum website for more information and additional packages available.</a><br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

	<div class="pf3a">

	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					Safety</h2>
			<h3 class="pt">
					Protection is great, prevention is better</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Our philosophy on safety emphasizes prevention with important features such as Active Handling and four-wheel antilock brakes, but in the event of a collision, Corvette convertible is engineered for safety before, during and — thanks to OnStar<sup>®</sup> — after a collision to help keep you <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">protected<sup>†</sup></a>.</p></div>
				</div></div>
<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_top">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 980px; top: 15px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 10px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Corvette%20Convertible/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-corvette-convertible-model-overview-cnt_well_1-318x117-25.png" alt="" width="318" height="117" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Corvette%20Convertible/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-corvette-convertible-model-overview-cnt_well_1-648x315-26.jpg" alt="" width="648" height="315" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h3 class="pt">
					Before</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Active Handling, run-flat tires and four-wheel antilock brakes help you stay on the road and in control to help avoid crashes in the first place, while standard xenon high-intensity discharge headlamps shed 900 lumens of light onto the road for excellent visibility. And if there’s a loss of tire pressure, Corvette convertible’s run-flat tires help enable safe function for some distance at a moderate speed until the tire can be repaired.</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h3 class="pt">
					During</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>In the event of a collision, Corvette convertible is designed to help keep you and your passengers protected with frontal and side-impact air <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_8" class="ln disclaimer_1">bags</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_8" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup>.<br>
</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h3 class="pt">
					After</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>OnStar with Directions &amp; Connections<sup>®</sup> and Automatic Crash <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">Response</a><sup><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-corvette-convertible_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">†</a></sup> uses built-in sensors that can automatically alert an Advisor who is immediately connected with your vehicle and can request emergency help be sent to your exact GPS location — even if you’re unable to respond. Standard for the first six months.<br>
</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>

									<div class="g-plusone" data-href="http://www.chevrolet.com/corvette-convertible.html" data-annotation="none" data-width="450" data-callback="googlePlusTracking"></div>
											</li>
							</ul>
			</dd>
		</dl>
	</div>
	</div>
</li><li><div class="cnt_btn_1 mod modCnt_btn_1 section mds-cmp-content02"><a href="/corvette-convertible/features-specs/trims.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'contentarea'});}" class="btn_sec"><span>See Features</span>
		</a></div>
</li></ul></div>
</div>
</div>
</div><div class="mds-area-pf1"><div class="cnt_well_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_well_1 mds-cmp-content20">
	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					How Sustainable is the Corvette?</h2>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Check out its “Ecologic” Features. Here at Chevrolet, we believe in being a responsible steward of our environment. Recently, we’ve developed a new way to communicate some of the environmentally significant features of each vehicle we make. We call it “Ecologic.”</p></div>
				</div></div>
<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05">
			<div class="inner">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared%20Resources/ecologic/2013-chevrolet-model-overview-ecologic-cnt-well-1-308x76-01.jpg" alt="" width="308" height="76" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Every aspect of Ecologic is audited by Two Tomorrows, an independent  third party sustainability auditor. To learn more about Ecologic and the  Two Tomorrows’ process, click here.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared%20Resources/ecologic/2013-chevrolet-model-overview-ecologic-cnt-well-1-648x315-02.jpg" alt="" width="648" height="315" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Fuel-Saving Technologies</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    Low-mass materials, such as an aluminum cockpit structure, lightweight composite body panels, balsa wood floor panel and an aluminum engine block and cylinder head, reduce engine workload and contribute to better fuel economy. </p>
<p>  A six-speed transmission allows the engine to operate at a lower rate of speed as compared to transmissions with fewer gears, which results in better fuel economy. Transmissions employ shift management technologies when maximum engine power is not required. When these technologies engage, engine workload is reduced, which contributes to better fuel economy. Manual transmission has skip shift technology (1st to 4th). Automatic transmission has 2nd gear start. </p>
<p>  </p>
<p>  The engine has been factory-filled with engine oil meeting GM's new dexos™ specification, which has improved viscosity characteristics as compared to the previous GF-4 oil, contributing to better fuel economy.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Responsible Manufacturing</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    The engine facilities are landfill-free. These facilities use a process to reuse, recycle or convert to energy all waste created in their daily operations, which conserves resources. Some water and engine-air deflectors are manufactured with more than 99% recycled content, which includes used tires. Recycled material conserves resources and reduces landfill deposits. </p>
<p>  </p>
<p>  The Toledo, OH, transmission facility (automatic transmission only) features a designated habitat area certified by the Wildlife Habitat Council, which provides ecological benefits.The Bowling Green, KY, assembly plant features solar charging canopies on the grounds, which conserves resources and lessens dependence on fossil fuels.</p>
<p>  Landfill gas supplies 16% of the energy to heat and cool the Toledo, OH, transmission facility (automatic transmission only), which makes the facility less reliant on fossil fuels.</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			End-of-Life Recyclability</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    After the vehicle’s useful life, 85% of it is recyclable. The majority of its components can be broken down and recycled, which conserves resources and reduces landfill deposits. </p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
</div>
